Overview\\nEnvoy v1.31.2 contains comprehensive access logging infrastructure spanning both sink implementations (access loggers) and filter implementations (access log filters). The system is designed to support multiple output formats, with significant JSON/structured logging support across most implementations.\\n\\n### Access Logger Sink Implementations\\n\\n#### 1. File Logger (envoy.access_loggers.file)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/file/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/file_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Full support)\\n- Supports multiple format options: `format` (text), `json_format` (JSON), `typed_json_format` (typed JSON), `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString)\\n- Implemented via `FileAccessLogFactory` which creates formatter instances using `SubstitutionFormatStringUtils`\\n- File logger writes formatted output directly to disk\\n\\n#### 2. Stream Loggers (envoy.access_loggers.stdout/stderr)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/config.cc`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured)\\n- Stdout/Stderr loggers support `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString)\\n- JSON formatting possible through SubstitutionFormatString configuration\\n- Implemented via `StdoutAccessLogFactory` and `StderrAccessLogFactory`\\n\\n#### 3. gRPC Access Log Service (ALS) - HTTP (envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_grpc_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured via Protocol Buffers)\\n- HTTP gRPC access logger sends HTTP request/response data via gRPC\\n- Supports custom tags (type.tracing.v3.CustomTag) for additional structured fields\\n- Implemented via `HttpGrpcAccessLogFactory`\\n- Proto includes HTTPRequestProperties and HTTPResponseProperties with headers/trailers\\n- Structured logging through protocol buffer messages to remote gRPC service\\n\\n#### 4. gRPC Access Log Service (ALS) - TCP (envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured via Protocol Buffers)\\n- TCP gRPC access logger sends TCP connection data via gRPC\\n- Uses CommonGrpcAccessLogConfig with streaming and custom tags\\n- Implemented via `TcpGrpcAccessLogFactory`\\n- Structured logging through protocol buffer messages\\n\\n#### 5. Fluentd Logger (envoy.access_loggers.fluentd)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/fluentd_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured)\\n- Sends logs to Fluentd via Forward Protocol over TCP\\n- Uses JSON formatter internally (`SubstitutionFormatStringUtils::createJsonFormatter`)\\n- Converts JSON to MessagePack for Fluentd wire format\\n- Supports nested JSON objects through `google.protobuf.Struct record` field\\n- Configured via `FluentdAccessLogFactory`\\n- Field: `record` is a Struct containing formatted fields rendered as strings, numbers, or booleans\\n\\n#### 6. OpenTelemetry Logger (envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured)\\n- Sends logs to OpenTelemetry Logs Collector via gRPC or HTTP\\n- Structured logging via OpenTelemetry proto format (LogResource)\\n- Supports `body` (AnyValue) and `attributes` (KeyValueList) for structured fields\\n- Supports custom tags (type.tracing.v3.CustomTag) for additional attributes\\n- Implemented via `AccessLogFactory` in open_telemetry namespace\\n- Can use both gRPC and HTTP/OTLP transports\\n\\n#### 7. WASM Logger (envoy.access_loggers.wasm)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/wasm_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** EXTENSIBLE (Depends on WASM plugin)\\n- Extensible logging via WASM plugin configuration\\n- Format and structure determined entirely by WASM plugin implementation\\n- Configured via `WasmAccessLogFactory`\\n- Allows custom logic for log processing and formatting\\n\\n### Access Logger Filter Implementations\\n\\nAll filters implement the `Filter` interface and are created through `FilterFactory::fromProto()` in `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.cc`. Filters are not sink implementations but determine whether logs are emitted:\\n\\n#### 1. StatusCodeFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on HTTP response status code comparison\\n- Supports: GE, EQ, LE operations\\n\\n#### 2. DurationFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on request/response duration comparison\\n- Supports: GE, EQ, LE operations\\n\\n#### 3. NotHealthCheckFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters out Envoy health check requests\\n\\n#### 4. Overview\\nEnvoy v1.31.2 contains comprehensive access logging infrastructure spanning both sink implementations (access loggers) and filter implementations (access log filters). The system is designed to support multiple output formats, with significant JSON/structured logging support across most implementations.\\n\\n### Access Logger Sink Implementations\\n\\n#### 1. File Logger (envoy.access_loggers.file)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/file/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/file_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Full support)\\n- Supports multiple format options: `format` (text), `json_format` (JSON), `typed_json_format` (typed JSON), `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString)\\n- Implemented via `FileAccessLogFactory` which creates formatter instances using `SubstitutionFormatStringUtils`\\n- File logger writes formatted output directly to disk\\n\\n#### 2. Stream Loggers (envoy.access_loggers.stdout/stderr)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/config.cc`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured)\\n- Stdout/Stderr loggers support `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString)\\n- JSON formatting possible through SubstitutionFormatString configuration\\n- Implemented via `StdoutAccessLogFactory` and `StderrAccessLogFactory`\\n\\n#### 3. gRPC Access Log Service (ALS) - HTTP (envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_grpc_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured via Protocol Buffers)\\n- HTTP gRPC access logger sends HTTP request/response data via gRPC\\n- Supports custom tags (type.tracing.v3.CustomTag) for additional structured fields\\n- Implemented via `HttpGrpcAccessLogFactory`\\n- Proto includes HTTPRequestProperties and HTTPResponseProperties with headers/trailers\\n- Structured logging through protocol buffer messages to remote gRPC service\\n\\n#### 4. gRPC Access Log Service (ALS) - TCP (envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured via Protocol Buffers)\\n- TCP gRPC access logger sends TCP connection data via gRPC\\n- Uses CommonGrpcAccessLogConfig with streaming and custom tags\\n- Implemented via `TcpGrpcAccessLogFactory`\\n- Structured logging through protocol buffer messages\\n\\n#### 5. Fluentd Logger (envoy.access_loggers.fluentd)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/fluentd_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured)\\n- Sends logs to Fluentd via Forward Protocol over TCP\\n- Uses JSON formatter internally (`SubstitutionFormatStringUtils::createJsonFormatter`)\\n- Converts JSON to MessagePack for Fluentd wire format\\n- Supports nested JSON objects through `google.protobuf.Struct record` field\\n- Configured via `FluentdAccessLogFactory`\\n- Field: `record` is a Struct containing formatted fields rendered as strings, numbers, or booleans\\n\\n#### 6. OpenTelemetry Logger (envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** YES (Structured)\\n- Sends logs to OpenTelemetry Logs Collector via gRPC or HTTP\\n- Structured logging via OpenTelemetry proto format (LogResource)\\n- Supports `body` (AnyValue) and `attributes` (KeyValueList) for structured fields\\n- Supports custom tags (type.tracing.v3.CustomTag) for additional attributes\\n- Implemented via `AccessLogFactory` in open_telemetry namespace\\n- Can use both gRPC and HTTP/OTLP transports\\n\\n#### 7. WASM Logger (envoy.access_loggers.wasm)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/wasm_access_log_impl.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`\\n**JSON Support:** EXTENSIBLE (Depends on WASM plugin)\\n- Extensible logging via WASM plugin configuration\\n- Format and structure determined entirely by WASM plugin implementation\\n- Configured via `WasmAccessLogFactory`\\n- Allows custom logic for log processing and formatting\\n\\n### Access Logger Filter Implementations\\n\\nAll filters implement the `Filter` interface and are created through `FilterFactory::fromProto()` in `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.cc`. Filters are not sink implementations but determine whether logs are emitted:\\n\\n#### 1. StatusCodeFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on HTTP response status code comparison\\n- Supports: GE, EQ, LE operations\\n\\n#### 2. DurationFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on request/response duration comparison\\n- Supports: GE, EQ, LE operations\\n\\n#### 3. NotHealthCheckFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters out Envoy health check requests\\n\\n#### 4. TraceableRequestFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters traceable requests only\\n\\n#### 5. RuntimeFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on runtime configuration and fractional percentages\\n\\n#### 6. AndFilter / OrFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Composite filters combining multiple filters with AND/OR logic\\n\\n#### 7. HeaderFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on HTTP header matching\\n\\n#### 8. ResponseFlagFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on Envoy response flags\\n\\n#### 9. GrpcStatusFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on gRPC status codes\\n- Can infer gRPC status from HTTP status codes\\n\\n#### 10. LogTypeFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on access log type (HTTP, TCP)\\n\\n#### 11. MetadataFilter\\n**Location:** `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.h`\\n- Filters based on dynamic metadata matching\\n\\n#### 12. CELAccessLogExtensionFilter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel)\\n**Location:** `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/config.cc` and `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/cel.h`\\n**Proto:** `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`\\n- Filters using Common Expression Language (CEL) expressions\\n- Evaluates expressions against Envoy attributes\\n- Requires USE_CEL_PARSER compile flag\\n- Supports complex filtering logic beyond built-in filters\\n\\n### Key Findings\\n\\n1. **JSON/Structured Logging Support:** 5 out of 7 sink implementations have explicit JSON support (File, Stream, HTTP gRPC, TCP gRPC, Fluentd, OpenTelemetry).
